Week 3: Webscraping

2024-09-18

1 Webscraping For Dummies: The Staff-Info Edition

So, we are going to do some good-good webscraping for dummies!

## List of 2
##  $ node:<externalptr> 
##  $ doc :<externalptr> 
##  - attr(*, "class")= chr [1:2] "xml_document" "xml_node"

Then we go to another department: Leiden’s Political Science Department

2 But What If I Want to Know More?

Well, sure we have some fun info about the names and positions of the staff. But how can we use this to do something with the information./ Let me tell you how you can use this! By using the names as starting points for setting up collaboration networks./ / Because we have these names, we can now use webscraping to find additional information associated with these names – such as the papers they have published, and with whom they have been published./ We do this by going to the OpenAlex API, and extracting our information of choice accordingly.

2.1 Get things started

2.3 Use the Wrapper

Because we are (weak), we are using the wrapper (becasue it’s easier)
Get the people first

First make separate objects for all their works

Then create one big object, in which we collect all four people’s work (all of ’em)

Then we create an adjacency matrix – first by filtering out the data from only the relevant years (2019 - 2023)

Then, we put all the information in a matrix – to create an adjacency matrix to assess patterns of collaboration
